\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} provides an interface for drawing, and how the drawing is clipped and transformed. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} contains a stack of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip values.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} together provide the state to draw into \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}}. Each \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} draw call transforms the geometry of the object by the concatenation of all \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} values in the stack. The transformed geometry is clipped by the intersection of all of clip values in the stack. The \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} draw calls use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} to supply drawing state such as color, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}}, text size, stroke width, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} and so on.

To draw to a pixel-\/based destination, create raster surface or G\+PU surface. Request \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} to obtain the interface to draw. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} generated by raster surface draws to memory visible to the C\+PU. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} generated by G\+PU surface uses Vulkan or Open\+GL to draw to the G\+PU.

To draw to a document, obtain \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} from S\+VG canvas, document P\+DF, or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture_recorder}{Sk\+Picture\+Recorder}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_document}{Sk\+Document}} based \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} and other \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} subclasses reference \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} describing the destination.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} can be constructed to draw to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} without first creating raster surface. This approach may be deprecated in the future.

Creates an empty \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} with no backing device or pixels, with a width and height of zero.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
empty \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}
\end{DoxyReturn}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_empty_constructor}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+empty\+\_\+constructor}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_adec6d012527048422c0bfa76b3e5b13e}\label{class_sk_canvas_adec6d012527048422c0bfa76b3e5b13e}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SkCanvas()}{SkCanvas()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/5]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Sk\+Canvas\+::\+Sk\+Canvas (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{width,  }\item[{int}]{height,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface_props}{Sk\+Surface\+Props}} $\ast$}]{props = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} of the specified dimensions without a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}}. Used by subclasses with custom implementations for draw member functions.

If props equals nullptr, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface_props}{Sk\+Surface\+Props}} are created with Sk\+Surface\+Props\+::\+Init\+Type settings, which choose the pixel striping direction and order. Since a platform may dynamically change its direction when the device is rotated, and since a platform may have multiple monitors with different characteristics, it is best not to rely on this legacy behavior.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em width} & zero or greater \\
\hline
{\em height} & zero or greater \\
\hline
{\em props} & L\+CD striping orientation and setting for device independent fonts; may be nullptr \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} placeholder with dimensions

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{accessTopLayerPixels()}{accessTopLayerPixels()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void $\ast$ Sk\+Canvas\+::access\+Top\+Layer\+Pixels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_image_info}{Sk\+Image\+Info}} $\ast$}]{info,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{row\+Bytes,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_i_point}{Sk\+I\+Point}} $\ast$}]{origin = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the pixel base address, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_image_info}{Sk\+Image\+Info}}, row\+Bytes, and origin if the pixels can be read directly. The returned address is only valid while \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is in scope and unchanged. Any \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} call or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} call may invalidate the returned address and other returned values.

If pixels are inaccessible, info, row\+Bytes, and origin are unchanged.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
address of pixels, or nullptr if inaccessible

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!accessTopRasterHandle@{accessTopRasterHandle}}
\index{accessTopRasterHandle@{accessTopRasterHandle}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{accessTopRasterHandle()}{accessTopRasterHandle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Sk\+Raster\+Handle\+Allocator\+::\+Handle Sk\+Canvas\+::access\+Top\+Raster\+Handle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}

Returns custom context that tracks the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip.

Use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_raster_handle_allocator}{Sk\+Raster\+Handle\+Allocator}} to blend Skia drawing with custom drawing, typically performed by the host platform user interface. The custom context returned is generated by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_raster_handle_allocator_ad5a06e782d7e4731b506f93ba360fefa}{Sk\+Raster\+Handle\+Allocator\+::\+Make\+Canvas}}, which creates a custom canvas with raster storage for the drawing destination.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
context of custom allocation
\end{DoxyReturn}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_accessTopRasterHandle}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+access\+Top\+Raster\+Handle}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a4048c03bae32364e8a660b5437e6a38c}\label{class_sk_canvas_a4048c03bae32364e8a660b5437e6a38c}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!androidFramework\_setDeviceClipRestriction@{androidFramework\_setDeviceClipRestriction}}
\index{androidFramework\_setDeviceClipRestriction@{androidFramework\_setDeviceClipRestriction}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{androidFramework\_setDeviceClipRestriction()}{androidFramework\_setDeviceClipRestriction()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::android\+Framework\+\_\+set\+Device\+Clip\+Restriction (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_i_rect}{Sk\+I\+Rect}} \&}]{rect }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the maximum clip rectangle, which can be set by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_afcefd4d2ac745ad086fd62f30bbd8564}{clip\+R\+Rect()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_abc79bd478516f398c31ae9f501154184}{clip\+Path()}} and intersect the current clip with the specified rect. The maximum clip affects only future clipping operations; it is not retroactive. The clip restriction is not recorded in pictures.

Pass an empty rect to disable maximum clip. This private A\+PI is for use by Android framework only.

D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED\+: Replace usage with Sk\+Android\+Framework\+Utils\+::replace\+Clip()


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em rect} & maximum allowed clip in device coordinates \\
\hline

\index{clipPath@{clipPath}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{clipPath()}{clipPath()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::clip\+Path (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} \&}]{path,  }\item[{bool}]{do\+Anti\+Alias = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Replaces clip with the intersection of clip and path. Resulting clip is aliased; pixels are fully contained by the clip. Sk\+Path\+::\+Fill\+Type determines if path describes the area inside or outside its contours; and if path contour overlaps itself or another path contour, whether the overlaps form part of the area. path is transformed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} before it is combined with clip.

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!discard@{discard}}
\index{discard@{discard}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{discard()}{discard()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::discard (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Makes \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} contents undefined. Subsequent calls that read \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels, such as drawing with Sk\+Blend\+Mode, return undefined results. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a4bd70c9638c294068b908347e87ccc7d}{discard()}} does not change clip or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a4bd70c9638c294068b908347e87ccc7d}{discard()}} may do nothing, depending on the implementation of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} that created \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a4bd70c9638c294068b908347e87ccc7d}{discard()}} allows optimized performance on subsequent draws by removing cached data associated with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}}. It is not necessary to call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a4bd70c9638c294068b908347e87ccc7d}{discard()}} once done with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}; any cached data is deleted when owning \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} is deleted. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_afdfa2c8f18412d979b7c0e6fbf658a74}\label{class_sk_canvas_afdfa2c8f18412d979b7c0e6fbf658a74}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawAnnotation@{drawAnnotation}}
\index{drawAnnotation@{drawAnnotation}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawAnnotation()}{drawAnnotation()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}

Only some canvas implementations, such as recording to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture}{Sk\+Picture}}, or drawing to document P\+DF, use annotations.

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawArc@{drawArc}}
\index{drawArc@{drawArc}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawArc()}{drawArc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Arc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} \&}]{oval,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{start\+Angle,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{sweep\+Angle,  }\item[{bool}]{use\+Center,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws arc using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

Arc is part of oval bounded by oval, sweeping from start\+Angle to start\+Angle plus sweep\+Angle. start\+Angle and sweep\+Angle are in degrees.

start\+Angle of zero places start point at the right middle edge of oval. A positive sweep\+Angle places arc end point clockwise from start point; a negative sweep\+Angle places arc end point counterclockwise from start point. sweep\+Angle may exceed 360 degrees, a full circle. If use\+Center is true, draw a wedge that includes lines from oval center to arc end points. If use\+Center is false, draw arc between end points.

If \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} oval is empty or sweep\+Angle is zero, nothing is drawn.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em oval} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} bounds of oval containing arc to draw \\
\hline
{\em start\+Angle} & angle in degrees where arc begins \\
\hline
{\em sweep\+Angle} & sweep angle in degrees; positive is clockwise \\
\hline
{\em use\+Center} & if true, include the center of the oval \\
\hline
{\em paint} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke or fill, blend, color, and so on, used to draw \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_ace6d74f7e43162984c184cac4edc4363}\label{class_sk_canvas_ace6d74f7e43162984c184cac4edc4363}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawAtlas@{drawAtlas}}
\index{drawAtlas@{drawAtlas}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawAtlas()}{drawAtlas()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Atlas (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image}{Sk\+Image}} $\ast$}]{atlas,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_r_s_xform}{Sk\+R\+S\+Xform}}}]{xform\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}}}]{tex\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_sk_color_8h_a84c81e6a24ff07a55333acf5603046a8}{Sk\+Color}}}]{colors\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{int}]{count,  }\item[{Sk\+Blend\+Mode}]{mode,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_sampling_options}{Sk\+Sampling\+Options}} \&}]{sampling,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} $\ast$}]{cull\+Rect,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} $\ast$}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a set of sprites from atlas, using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and optional \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint. paint uses anti-\/alias, alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and Sk\+Blend\+Mode to draw, if present. For each entry in the array, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} tex locates sprite in atlas, and \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_r_s_xform}{Sk\+R\+S\+Xform}} xform transforms it into destination space.

xform, tex, and colors if present, must contain count entries. Optional colors are applied for each sprite using Sk\+Blend\+Mode mode, treating sprite as source and colors as destination. Optional cull\+Rect is a conservative bounds of all transformed sprites. If cull\+Rect is outside of clip, canvas can skip drawing.

If atlas is nullptr, this draws nothing.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em atlas} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image}{Sk\+Image}} containing sprites \\
\hline
{\em xform} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_r_s_xform}{Sk\+R\+S\+Xform}} mappings for sprites in atlas \\
\hline
{\em tex} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} locations of sprites in atlas \\
\hline
{\em colors} & one per sprite, blended with sprite using Sk\+Blend\+Mode; may be nullptr \\
\hline
{\em count} & number of sprites to draw \\
\hline
{\em mode} & Sk\+Blend\+Mode combining colors and sprites \\
\hline
{\em sampling} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_sampling_options}{Sk\+Sampling\+Options}} used when sampling from the atlas image \\
\hline
{\em cull\+Rect} & bounds of transformed sprites for efficient clipping; may be nullptr \\
\hline
{\em paint} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, Sk\+Blend\+Mode, and so on; may be nullptr \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_ad70b82e3a846bba5a625e7aca15d4359}\label{class_sk_canvas_ad70b82e3a846bba5a625e7aca15d4359}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawCircle@{drawCircle}}

In paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} determines if circle is stroked or filled; if stroked, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width describes the line thickness.

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawDrawable@{drawDrawable}}
\index{drawDrawable@{drawDrawable}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawDrawable()}{drawDrawable()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Drawable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_drawable}{Sk\+Drawable}} $\ast$}]{drawable,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} $\ast$}]{matrix = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_drawable}{Sk\+Drawable}} drawable using clip and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, concatenated with optional matrix.

If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} has an asynchronous implementation, as is the case when it is recording into \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture}{Sk\+Picture}}, then drawable will be referenced, so that \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_drawable_ade63adbce24872944c202e3cb619359b}{Sk\+Drawable\+::draw()}} can be called when the operation is finalized. To force immediate drawing, call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_drawable_ade63adbce24872944c202e3cb619359b}{Sk\+Drawable\+::draw()}} instead.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em drawable} & custom struct encapsulating drawing commands \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawDrawable()}{drawDrawable()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Drawable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_drawable}{Sk\+Drawable}} $\ast$}]{drawable,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{x,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_drawable}{Sk\+Drawable}} drawable using clip and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, offset by (x, y).

If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} has an asynchronous implementation, as is the case when it is recording into \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture}{Sk\+Picture}}, then drawable will be referenced, so that \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_drawable_ade63adbce24872944c202e3cb619359b}{Sk\+Drawable\+::draw()}} can be called when the operation is finalized. To force immediate drawing, call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_drawable_ade63adbce24872944c202e3cb619359b}{Sk\+Drawable\+::draw()}} instead.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_drawDrawable_2}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+draw\+Drawable\+\_\+2}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_ad7149e359d4d0cfd2ad708e905f0d8c6}\label{class_sk_canvas_ad7149e359d4d0cfd2ad708e905f0d8c6}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawDRRect@{drawDRRect}}
\index{drawDRRect@{drawDRRect}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawDRRect()}{drawDRRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+D\+R\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} \&}]{outer,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} \&}]{inner,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} outer and inner using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint. outer must contain inner or the drawing is undefined. In paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} determines if \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} is stroked or filled; if stroked, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width describes the line thickness. If stroked and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} corner has zero length radii, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_ac582b0cbf59909c9056de34a6b977cca}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Join}} can draw corners rounded or square.

G\+P\+U-\/backed platforms optimize drawing when both outer and inner are concave and outer contains inner. These platforms may not be able to draw \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} built with identical data as fast.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em outer} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} outer bounds to draw \\
\hline
{\em inner} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} inner bounds to draw \\
\hline
{\em paint} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke or fill, blend, color, and so on, used to draw\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_drawDRRect_a}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+draw\+D\+R\+Rect\+\_\+a}} example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_drawDRRect_b}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+draw\+D\+R\+Rect\+\_\+b}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a8cefe226459f3787b5f1eea25c433dc4}\label{class_sk_canvas_a8cefe226459f3787b5f1eea25c433dc4}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawGlyphs()}{drawGlyphs()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Glyphs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{count,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_sk_types_8h_a1d5e8bd1d16e0484508ec693933b0a54}{Sk\+Glyph\+ID}}}]{glyphs\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{positions\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{clusters\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{int}]{text\+Byte\+Count,  }\item[{const char}]{utf8text\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{origin,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_font}{Sk\+Font}} \&}]{font,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws count glyphs, at positions relative to origin styled with font and paint with supporting utf8 and cluster information.

This function draw glyphs at the given positions relative to the given origin. It does not perform typeface fallback for glyphs not found in the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}} in font.

The drawing obeys the current transform matrix and clipping.

All elements of paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path_effect}{Sk\+Path\+Effect}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}; apply to text. By default, draws filled black glyphs.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawGlyphs()}{drawGlyphs()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Glyphs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{count,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_sk_types_8h_a1d5e8bd1d16e0484508ec693933b0a54}{Sk\+Glyph\+ID}}}]{glyphs\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_r_s_xform}{Sk\+R\+S\+Xform}}}]{xforms\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{origin,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_font}{Sk\+Font}} \&}]{font,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws count glyphs, at positions relative to origin styled with font and paint.

This function draw glyphs using the given scaling and rotations. They are positioned relative to the given origin. It does not perform typeface fallback for glyphs not found in the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}} in font.

The drawing obeys the current transform matrix and clipping.

All elements of paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path_effect}{Sk\+Path\+Effect}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}; apply to text. By default, draws filled black glyphs.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_ab8a724321360f9f71b409f8d11172628}\label{class_sk_canvas_ab8a724321360f9f71b409f8d11172628}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawImageLattice@{drawImageLattice}}
\index{drawImageLattice@{drawImageLattice}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawImageLattice()}{drawImageLattice()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Image\+Lattice (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image}{Sk\+Image}} $\ast$}]{image,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_canvas_1_1_lattice}{Lattice}} \&}]{lattice,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} \&}]{dst,  }\item[{Sk\+Filter\+Mode}]{filter,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} $\ast$}]{paint = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image}{Sk\+Image}} image stretched proportionally to fit into \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} dst.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_canvas_1_1_lattice}{Sk\+Canvas\+::\+Lattice}} lattice divides image into a rectangular grid. Each intersection of an even-\/numbered row and column is fixed; fixed lattice elements never scale larger than their initial size and shrink proportionately when all fixed elements exceed the bitmap dimension. All other grid elements scale to fill the available space, if any.

Additionally transform draw using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and optional \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint is supplied, apply \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and Sk\+Blend\+Mode. If image is k\+Alpha\+\_\+8\+\_\+\+Sk\+Color\+Type, apply \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}. If paint contains \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}}, generate mask from image bounds. Any \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}} on paint is ignored as is paint anti-\/aliasing state.

If generated mask extends beyond bitmap bounds, replicate bitmap edge colors, just as \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} made from Sk\+Shader\+::\+Make\+Bitmap\+Shader with Sk\+Shader\+::k\+Clamp\+\_\+\+Tile\+Mode set replicates the bitmap edge color when it samples outside of its bounds.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em image} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image}{Sk\+Image}} containing pixels, dimensions, and format \\
\hline
{\em lattice} & division of bitmap into fixed and variable rectangles \\
\hline
{\em dst} & destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} of image to draw to \\
\hline
{\em filter} & what technique to use when sampling the image \\
\hline
{\em paint} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} containing Sk\+Blend\+Mode, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and so on; or nullptr \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a3a9a10b43dcffdac586ca21b853627b3}\label{class_sk_canvas_a3a9a10b43dcffdac586ca21b853627b3}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawImageNine@{drawImageNine}}
\index{drawImageNine@{drawImageNine}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawImageNine()}{drawImageNine()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Image\+Nine (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image}{Sk\+Image}} $\ast$}]{image,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_i_rect}{Sk\+I\+Rect}} \&}]{center,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} \&}]{dst,  }\item[{Sk\+Filter\+Mode}]{filter,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} $\ast$}]{paint = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image}{Sk\+Image}} image stretched proportionally to fit into \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} dst. \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_i_rect}{Sk\+I\+Rect}} center divides the image into nine sections\+: four sides, four corners, and the center. Corners are unmodified or scaled down proportionately if their sides are larger than dst; center and four sides are scaled to fit remaining space, if any.

Additionally transform draw using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and optional \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint is supplied, apply \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and Sk\+Blend\+Mode. If image is k\+Alpha\+\_\+8\+\_\+\+Sk\+Color\+Type, apply \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}. If paint contains \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}}, generate mask from image bounds. Any \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}} on paint is ignored as is paint anti-\/aliasing state.

If generated mask extends beyond image bounds, replicate image edge colors, just as \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} made from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_a74353e5b80ca5efdaf51a11755149aba}{Sk\+Image\+::make\+Shader}} with Sk\+Shader\+::k\+Clamp\+\_\+\+Tile\+Mode set replicates the image edge color when it samples outside of its bounds.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em image} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image}{Sk\+Image}} containing pixels, dimensions, and format \\
\hline
{\em center} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_i_rect}{Sk\+I\+Rect}} edge of image corners and sides \\
\hline
{\em dst} & destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} of image to draw to \\
\hline
{\em filter} & what technique to use when sampling the image \\
\hline
{\em paint} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} containing Sk\+Blend\+Mode, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and so on; or nullptr \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{drawPatch@{drawPatch}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawPatch()}{drawPatch()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Patch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{cubics\mbox{[}12\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_sk_color_8h_a84c81e6a24ff07a55333acf5603046a8}{Sk\+Color}}}]{colors\mbox{[}4\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{tex\+Coords\mbox{[}4\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} cubic Coons patch\+: the interpolation of four cubics with shared corners, associating a color, and optionally a texture \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}, with each corner.

Coons patch uses clip and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, paint \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and Sk\+Blend\+Mode. If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} is provided it is treated as Coons patch texture; Sk\+Blend\+Mode mode combines color colors and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} if both are provided.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}} array cubics specifies four \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} cubic starting at the top-\/left corner, in clockwise order, sharing every fourth point. The last \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} cubic ends at the first point.

Color array color associates colors with corners in top-\/left, top-\/right, bottom-\/right, bottom-\/left order.

If paint contains \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}} array tex\+Coords maps \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} as texture to corners in top-\/left, top-\/right, bottom-\/right, bottom-\/left order. If tex\+Coords is nullptr, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} is mapped using positions (derived from cubics).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em cubics} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} cubic array, sharing common points \\
\hline
{\em colors} & color array, one for each corner \\
\hline
{\em tex\+Coords} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}} array of texture coordinates, mapping \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} to corners; may be nullptr \\
\hline
{\em paint} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, Sk\+Blend\+Mode, used to draw \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a29b048324b32bfc785c0c256d65aa885}\label{class_sk_canvas_a29b048324b32bfc785c0c256d65aa885}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawPatch()}{drawPatch()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Patch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{cubics\mbox{[}12\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_sk_color_8h_a84c81e6a24ff07a55333acf5603046a8}{Sk\+Color}}}]{colors\mbox{[}4\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{tex\+Coords\mbox{[}4\mbox{]},  }\item[{Sk\+Blend\+Mode}]{mode,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a Coons patch\+: the interpolation of four cubics with shared corners, associating a color, and optionally a texture \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}, with each corner.

Coons patch uses clip and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, paint \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and Sk\+Blend\+Mode. If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} is provided it is treated as Coons patch texture; Sk\+Blend\+Mode mode combines color colors and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} if both are provided.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}} array cubics specifies four \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} cubic starting at the top-\/left corner, in clockwise order, sharing every fourth point. The last \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} cubic ends at the first point.

Color array color associates colors with corners in top-\/left, top-\/right, bottom-\/right, bottom-\/left order.

If paint contains \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}} array tex\+Coords maps \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} as texture to corners in top-\/left, top-\/right, bottom-\/right, bottom-\/left order. If tex\+Coords is nullptr, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}} is mapped using positions (derived from cubics).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawPath()}{drawPath()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Path (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} \&}]{path,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} path using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} contains an array of path contour, each of which may be open or closed.

In paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} determines if \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} is stroked or filled\+: if filled, Sk\+Path\+::\+Fill\+Type determines whether path contour describes inside or outside of fill; if stroked, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width describes the line thickness, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Cap}} describes line ends, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_ac582b0cbf59909c9056de34a6b977cca}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Join}} describes how corners are drawn.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em path} & \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path}{Sk\+Path}} to draw \\
\hline
{\em paint} & stroke, blend, color, and so on, used to draw\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Picture (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classsk__sp}{sk\+\_\+sp}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture}{Sk\+Picture}} $>$ \&}]{picture,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} $\ast$}]{matrix,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} $\ast$}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture}{Sk\+Picture}} picture, using clip and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}; transforming picture with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} matrix, if provided; and use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and Sk\+Blend\+Mode, if provided.

If paint is non-\/null, then the picture is always drawn into a temporary layer before actually landing on the canvas. Note that drawing into a layer can also change its appearance if there are any non-\/associative blend\+Modes inside any of the pictures elements.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawPoint()}{drawPoint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Point (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{p,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Draws point p using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

The shape of point drawn depends on paint \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Cap}}. If paint is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333ab00b95302fe33924e63513c82b53f16b}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Round\+\_\+\+Cap}}, draw a circle of diameter \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width. If paint is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333ada3bff894a3c2a8874860e533bc04334}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Square\+\_\+\+Cap}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333abaac9668fb0acc014c962d843d6674b5}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Butt\+\_\+\+Cap}}, draw a square of width and height \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} is ignored, as if were set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fda4bcc9f35fd6468ad92012c70daf7a495}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Stroke\+\_\+\+Style}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawPoint()}{drawPoint()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Point (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{x,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{y,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws point at (x, y) using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

If paint is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333ab00b95302fe33924e63513c82b53f16b}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Round\+\_\+\+Cap}}, draw a circle of diameter \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width. If paint is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333ada3bff894a3c2a8874860e533bc04334}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Square\+\_\+\+Cap}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333abaac9668fb0acc014c962d843d6674b5}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Butt\+\_\+\+Cap}}, draw a square of width and height \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} is ignored, as if were set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fda4bcc9f35fd6468ad92012c70daf7a495}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Stroke\+\_\+\+Style}}.

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawPoints@{drawPoints}}
\index{drawPoints@{drawPoints}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawPoints()}{drawPoints()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Points (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_af1bcd412326a6886e0f260d4d2dc757b}{Point\+Mode}}}]{mode,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{count,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{pts\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws pts using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint. count is the number of points; if count is less than one, has no effect. mode may be one of\+: k\+Points\+\_\+\+Point\+Mode, k\+Lines\+\_\+\+Point\+Mode, or k\+Polygon\+\_\+\+Point\+Mode.

If mode is k\+Points\+\_\+\+Point\+Mode, the shape of point drawn depends on paint \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Cap}}. If paint is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333ab00b95302fe33924e63513c82b53f16b}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Round\+\_\+\+Cap}}, each point draws a circle of diameter \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width. If paint is set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333ada3bff894a3c2a8874860e533bc04334}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Square\+\_\+\+Cap}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333abaac9668fb0acc014c962d843d6674b5}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Butt\+\_\+\+Cap}}, each point draws a square of width and height \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width.

If mode is k\+Lines\+\_\+\+Point\+Mode, each pair of points draws a line segment. One line is drawn for every two points; each point is used once. If count is odd, the final point is ignored.

If mode is k\+Polygon\+\_\+\+Point\+Mode, each adjacent pair of points draws a line segment. count minus one lines are drawn; the first and last point are used once.

Each line segment respects paint \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a0f78de8559b795defba93171f6cb6333}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Cap}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} is ignored, as if were set to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fda4bcc9f35fd6468ad92012c70daf7a495}{Sk\+Paint\+::k\+Stroke\+\_\+\+Style}}.

Always draws each element one at a time; is not affected by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_ac582b0cbf59909c9056de34a6b977cca}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Join}}, and unlike \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_acddf41dddcd12333b061ce9c963616bb}{draw\+Path()}}, does not create a mask from all points and lines before drawing.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode} & whether pts draws points or lines \\
\hline
{\em count} & number of points in the array \\
\hline
{\em pts} & array of points to draw \\
\hline
{\em paint} & stroke, blend, color, and so on, used to draw\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_drawPoints}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+draw\+Points}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a15a77a3479b8f8731442d4a4ea2772b3}\label{class_sk_canvas_a15a77a3479b8f8731442d4a4ea2772b3}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawRect@{drawRect}}
\index{drawRect@{drawRect}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawRect()}{drawRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} \&}]{rect,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} rect using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint. In paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} determines if rectangle is stroked or filled; if stroked, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width describes the line thickness, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_ac582b0cbf59909c9056de34a6b977cca}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Join}} draws the corners rounded or square.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em rect} & rectangle to draw \\
\hline
{\em paint} & stroke or fill, blend, color, and so on, used to draw\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Region (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_region}{Sk\+Region}} \&}]{region,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_region}{Sk\+Region}} region using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint. In paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} determines if rectangle is stroked or filled; if stroked, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width describes the line thickness, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_ac582b0cbf59909c9056de34a6b977cca}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Join}} draws the corners rounded or square.

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawRoundRect@{drawRoundRect}}
\index{drawRoundRect@{drawRoundRect}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawRoundRect()}{drawRoundRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Round\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} \&}]{rect,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{rx,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{ry,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} bounded by \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} rect, with corner radii (rx, ry) using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

In paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} determines if \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} is stroked or filled; if stroked, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width describes the line thickness. If rx or ry are less than zero, they are treated as if they are zero. If rx plus ry exceeds rect width or rect height, radii are scaled down to fit. If rx and ry are zero, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} is drawn as \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} and if stroked is affected by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_ac582b0cbf59909c9056de34a6b977cca}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Join}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em rect} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} bounds of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} to draw \\
\hline
{\em rx} & axis length on x-\/axis of oval describing rounded corners \\
\hline
{\em ry} & axis length on y-\/axis of oval describing rounded corners \\
\hline
{\em paint} & stroke, blend, color, and so on, used to draw\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_drawRoundRect}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+draw\+Round\+Rect}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_ab50290cf9da84da457652d73ea09c0f5}\label{class_sk_canvas_ab50290cf9da84da457652d73ea09c0f5}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+R\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} \&}]{rrect,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_r_rect}{Sk\+R\+Rect}} rrect using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint. In paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint_a6f5b4ff088821b2940b148dd4cb6b9fd}{Sk\+Paint\+::\+Style}} determines if rrect is stroked or filled; if stroked, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} stroke width describes the line thickness.

rrect may represent a rectangle, circle, oval, uniformly rounded rectangle, or may have any combination of positive non-\/square radii for the four corners.

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!drawSimpleText@{drawSimpleText}}
\index{drawSimpleText@{drawSimpleText}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{drawSimpleText()}{drawSimpleText()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Simple\+Text (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{text,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{byte\+Length,  }\item[{Sk\+Text\+Encoding}]{encoding,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{x,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{y,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_font}{Sk\+Font}} \&}]{font,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws text, with origin at (x, y), using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_font}{Sk\+Font}} font, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

When encoding is Sk\+Text\+Encoding\+::k\+U\+T\+F8, Sk\+Text\+Encoding\+::k\+U\+T\+F16, or Sk\+Text\+Encoding\+::k\+U\+T\+F32, this function uses the default character-\/to-\/glyph mapping from the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}} in font. It does not perform typeface fallback for characters not found in the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}}. It does not perform kerning or other complex shaping; glyphs are positioned based on their default advances.

Text meaning depends on Sk\+Text\+Encoding.

Text size is affected by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_font}{Sk\+Font}} text size. Default text size is 12 point.

All elements of paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path_effect}{Sk\+Path\+Effect}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}; apply to text. By default, draws filled black glyphs.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em text} & character code points or glyphs drawn \\
\hline
{\em byte\+Length} & byte length of text array \\
\hline
{\em encoding} & text encoding used in the text array \\
\hline
{\em x} & start of text on x-\/axis \\
\hline
{\em y} & start of text on y-\/axis \\
\hline
{\em font} & typeface, text size and so, used to describe the text \\
\hline
{\em paint} & blend, color, and so on, used to draw \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_ae280406fb774e5a8bffbeaf3f1c927e7}\label{class_sk_canvas_ae280406fb774e5a8bffbeaf3f1c927e7}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+String (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char}]{str\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{x,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{y,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_font}{Sk\+Font}} \&}]{font,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Draws null terminated string, with origin at (x, y), using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_font}{Sk\+Font}} font, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

This function uses the default character-\/to-\/glyph mapping from the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}} in font. It does not perform typeface fallback for characters not found in the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}}. It does not perform kerning; glyphs are positioned based on their default advances.

String str is encoded as U\+T\+F-\/8.

Text size is affected by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and font text size. Default text size is 12 point.

All elements of paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path_effect}{Sk\+Path\+Effect}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}; apply to text. By default, draws filled black glyphs.

It does not perform typeface fallback for characters not found in the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}}. Text size is affected by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_font}{Sk\+Font}} text size. Default text size is 12 point.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::draw\+Text\+Blob (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classsk__sp}{sk\+\_\+sp}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_text_blob}{Sk\+Text\+Blob}} $>$ \&}]{blob,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{x,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{y,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} \&}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Draws \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_text_blob}{Sk\+Text\+Blob}} blob at (x, y), using clip, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint.

blob contains glyphs, their positions, and paint attributes specific to text\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_typeface}{Sk\+Typeface}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} text size, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} text scale x, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} text skew x, Sk\+Paint\+::\+Align, Sk\+Paint\+::\+Hinting, anti-\/alias, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} fake bold, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} font embedded bitmaps, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} full hinting spacing, L\+CD text, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} linear text, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} subpixel text.

Sk\+Text\+Encoding must be set to Sk\+Text\+Encoding\+::k\+Glyph\+ID.

Elements of paint\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_path_effect}{Sk\+Path\+Effect}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_mask_filter}{Sk\+Mask\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}; apply to blob.

If vertices colors are defined in vertices, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint contains \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}, Sk\+Blend\+Mode mode combines vertices colors with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_shader}{Sk\+Shader}}.

\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_drawVertices}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+draw\+Vertices}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_aa9e1a224a23c880db7ef8022adaf6480}\label{class_sk_canvas_aa9e1a224a23c880db7ef8022adaf6480}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!experimental\_DrawEdgeAAImageSet@{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAImageSet}}
\index{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAImageSet@{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAImageSet}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAImageSet()}{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAImageSet()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::experimental\+\_\+\+Draw\+Edge\+A\+A\+Image\+Set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_canvas_1_1_image_set_entry}{Image\+Set\+Entry}}}]{image\+Set\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{int}]{cnt,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{dst\+Clips\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}}]{pre\+View\+Matrices\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]},  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_sampling_options}{Sk\+Sampling\+Options}} \&}]{sampling,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} $\ast$}]{paint = {\ttfamily nullptr},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8997239ed4fd8e08bf4b66b3f6eeb40c}{Src\+Rect\+Constraint}}}]{constraint = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8997239ed4fd8e08bf4b66b3f6eeb40ca33a44e18142c9cd28f2b76b7d5f7bc9e}{k\+Strict\+\_\+\+Src\+Rect\+Constraint}}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is an bulk variant of \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8e5d4fc04417355ca0d23feafcd81ac3}{experimental\+\_\+\+Draw\+Edge\+A\+A\+Quad()}} that renders \textquotesingle{}cnt\textquotesingle{} textured quads. For each entry, \textquotesingle{}f\+Dst\+Rect\textquotesingle{} is rendered with its clip (determined by entry\textquotesingle{}s \textquotesingle{}f\+Has\+Clip\textquotesingle{} and the current index in \textquotesingle{}dst\+Clip\textquotesingle{}). The entry\textquotesingle{}s f\+Image is applied to the destination rectangle by sampling from \textquotesingle{}f\+Src\+Rect\textquotesingle{} sub-\/image. The corners of \textquotesingle{}f\+Src\+Rect\textquotesingle{} map to the corners of \textquotesingle{}f\+Dst\+Rect\textquotesingle{}, just like in draw\+Image\+Rect(), and they will be properly interpolated when applying a clip.

Like \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8e5d4fc04417355ca0d23feafcd81ac3}{experimental\+\_\+\+Draw\+Edge\+A\+A\+Quad()}}, each entry can specify edge AA flags that apply to both the destination rect and its clip.

If provided, the \textquotesingle{}dst\+Clips\textquotesingle{} array must have length equal 4 $\ast$ the number of entries with f\+Has\+Clip true. If \textquotesingle{}dst\+Clips\textquotesingle{} is null, every entry must have \textquotesingle{}f\+Has\+Clip\textquotesingle{} set to false. The destination clip coordinates will be read consecutively with the image set entries, advancing by 4 points every time an entry with f\+Has\+Clip is passed.

This entry point supports per-\/entry manipulations to the canvas\textquotesingle{}s current matrix. If an entry provides \textquotesingle{}f\+Matrix\+Index\textquotesingle{} $>$= 0, it will be drawn as if the canvas\textquotesingle{}s C\+TM was canvas-\/$>$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ab5d3c67a63129f42692d6cb4fb75db23}{get\+Total\+Matrix()}} $\ast$ pre\+View\+Matrices\mbox{[}f\+Matrix\+Index\mbox{]}. If \textquotesingle{}f\+Matrix\+Index\textquotesingle{} is less than 0, the pre-\/view matrix transform is implicitly the identity, so it will be drawn using just the current canvas matrix. The pre-\/view matrix modifies the canvas\textquotesingle{}s view matrix, it does not affect the local coordinates of each entry.

An optional paint may be provided, which supports the same subset of features usable with draw\+Image\+Rect (i.\+e. assumed to be filled and no path effects). When a paint is provided, the image set is drawn as if each image used the applied paint independently, so each is affected by the image, color, and/or mask filter. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a8e5d4fc04417355ca0d23feafcd81ac3}\label{class_sk_canvas_a8e5d4fc04417355ca0d23feafcd81ac3}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!experimental\_DrawEdgeAAQuad@{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAQuad}}
\index{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAQuad@{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAQuad}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAQuad()}{experimental\_DrawEdgeAAQuad()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::experimental\+\_\+\+Draw\+Edge\+A\+A\+Quad (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} \&}]{rect,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_point}{Sk\+Point}}}]{clip\mbox{[}4\mbox{]},  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_af71b7245651dfa4a873a23336fafec48}{Quad\+A\+A\+Flags}}}]{aa\+Flags,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_color4f}{Sk\+Color4f}} \&}]{color,  }\item[{Sk\+Blend\+Mode}]{mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is an experimental A\+PI for the Skia\+Renderer Chromium project, and its A\+PI will surely evolve if it is not removed outright.

This behaves very similarly to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a15a77a3479b8f8731442d4a4ea2772b3}{draw\+Rect()}} combined with a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_abc79bd478516f398c31ae9f501154184}{clip\+Path()}} formed by clip quadrilateral. \textquotesingle{}rect\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}clip\textquotesingle{} are in the same coordinate space. If \textquotesingle{}clip\textquotesingle{} is null, then it is as if the rectangle was not clipped (or, alternatively, clipped to itself). If not null, then it must provide 4 points.

In addition to combining the draw and clipping into one operation, this function adds the additional capability of controlling each of the rectangle\textquotesingle{}s edges anti-\/aliasing independently. The edges of the clip will respect the per-\/edge AA flags. It is required that \textquotesingle{}clip\textquotesingle{} be contained inside \textquotesingle{}rect\textquotesingle{}. In terms of mapping to edge labels, the \textquotesingle{}clip\textquotesingle{} points should be ordered top-\/left, top-\/right, bottom-\/right, bottom-\/left so that the edge between \mbox{[}0\mbox{]} and \mbox{[}1\mbox{]} is \char`\"{}top\char`\"{}, \mbox{[}1\mbox{]} and \mbox{[}2\mbox{]} is \char`\"{}right\char`\"{}, \mbox{[}2\mbox{]} and \mbox{[}3\mbox{]} is \char`\"{}bottom\char`\"{}, and \mbox{[}3\mbox{]} and \mbox{[}0\mbox{]} is \char`\"{}left\char`\"{}. This ordering matches \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect_a1c64f14d3855d1947aa48e7cc7c9ba1f}{Sk\+Rect\+::to\+Quad()}}.

This A\+PI only draws solid color, filled rectangles so it does not accept a full \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a3f8ea661c6021dc4dde325aab87870bf}\label{class_sk_canvas_a3f8ea661c6021dc4dde325aab87870bf}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!flush@{flush}}
\index{flush@{flush}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{flush()}{flush()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::flush (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Triggers the immediate execution of all pending draw operations. If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is associated with G\+PU surface, resolves all pending G\+PU operations. If \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is associated with raster surface, has no effect; raster draw operations are never deferred.

D\+E\+P\+R\+E\+C\+A\+T\+ED\+: Replace usage with Gr\+Direct\+Context\+::flush() \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a6bf0f33cbdde5b0c90a2395d1ba14a8b}\label{class_sk_canvas_a6bf0f33cbdde5b0c90a2395d1ba14a8b}}

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!MakeRasterDirect@{MakeRasterDirect}}
\index{MakeRasterDirect@{MakeRasterDirect}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MakeRasterDirect()}{MakeRasterDirect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} $>$ Sk\+Canvas\+::\+Make\+Raster\+Direct (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_image_info}{Sk\+Image\+Info}} \&}]{info,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{pixels,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{row\+Bytes,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface_props}{Sk\+Surface\+Props}} $\ast$}]{props = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}

Allocates raster \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} that will draw directly into pixels.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is returned if all parameters are valid. Valid parameters include\+: info dimensions are zero or positive; info contains Sk\+Color\+Type and Sk\+Alpha\+Type supported by raster surface; pixels is not nullptr; row\+Bytes is zero or large enough to contain info width pixels of Sk\+Color\+Type.

Pass zero for row\+Bytes to compute row\+Bytes from info width and size of pixel. If row\+Bytes is greater than zero, it must be equal to or greater than info width times bytes required for Sk\+Color\+Type.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_pixel}{Pixel}} buffer size should be info height times computed row\+Bytes. Pixels are not initialized. To access pixels after drawing, call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a3f8ea661c6021dc4dde325aab87870bf}{flush()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a1da746e87186d5e3fc0b4838f782e1c4}{peek\+Pixels()}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em info} & width, height, Sk\+Color\+Type, Sk\+Alpha\+Type, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_space}{Sk\+Color\+Space}}, of raster surface; width, or height, or both, may be zero \\
\hline
{\em pixels} & pointer to destination pixels buffer \\
\hline
{\em row\+Bytes} & interval from one \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} row to the next, or zero \\
\hline
{\em props} & L\+CD striping orientation and setting for device independent fonts; may be nullptr \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} if all parameters are valid; otherwise, nullptr 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a00b50eebd3b47ae6f371a2c7af2a9f01}\label{class_sk_canvas_a00b50eebd3b47ae6f371a2c7af2a9f01}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!MakeRasterDirectN32@{MakeRasterDirectN32}}
\index{MakeRasterDirectN32@{MakeRasterDirectN32}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MakeRasterDirectN32()}{MakeRasterDirectN32()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static std\+::unique\+\_\+ptr$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}$>$ Sk\+Canvas\+::\+Make\+Raster\+Direct\+N32 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{width,  }\item[{int}]{height,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_sk_color_8h_a9ec12bd74c4b63b5da802b419106b8ea}{Sk\+P\+M\+Color}} $\ast$}]{pixels,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{row\+Bytes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [static]}}

Allocates raster \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} specified by inline image specification. Subsequent \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} calls draw into pixels. Sk\+Color\+Type is set to k\+N32\+\_\+\+Sk\+Color\+Type. Sk\+Alpha\+Type is set to k\+Premul\+\_\+\+Sk\+Alpha\+Type. To access pixels after drawing, call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a3f8ea661c6021dc4dde325aab87870bf}{flush()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a1da746e87186d5e3fc0b4838f782e1c4}{peek\+Pixels()}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is returned if all parameters are valid. Valid parameters include\+: width and height are zero or positive; pixels is not nullptr; row\+Bytes is zero or large enough to contain width pixels of k\+N32\+\_\+\+Sk\+Color\+Type.

Pass zero for row\+Bytes to compute row\+Bytes from width and size of pixel. If row\+Bytes is greater than zero, it must be equal to or greater than width times bytes required for Sk\+Color\+Type.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_pixel}{Pixel}} buffer size should be height times row\+Bytes.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em width} & pixel column count on raster surface created; must be zero or greater \\
\hline
{\em height} & pixel row count on raster surface created; must be zero or greater \\
\hline
{\em pixels} & pointer to destination pixels buffer; buffer size should be height times row\+Bytes \\
\hline
{\em row\+Bytes} & interval from one \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} row to the next, or zero \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} if all parameters are valid; otherwise, nullptr 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classsk__sp}{sk\+\_\+sp}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} $>$ Sk\+Canvas\+::make\+Surface (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_image_info}{Sk\+Image\+Info}} \&}]{info,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface_props}{Sk\+Surface\+Props}} $\ast$}]{props = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} matching info and props, and associates it with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}. Returns nullptr if no match found.

If props is nullptr, matches \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface_props}{Sk\+Surface\+Props}} in \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}. If props is nullptr and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} does not have \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface_props}{Sk\+Surface\+Props}}, creates \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} with default \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface_props}{Sk\+Surface\+Props}}.

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!markCTM@{markCTM}}
\index{markCTM@{markCTM}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{markCTM()}{markCTM()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::mark\+C\+TM (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const char $\ast$}]{name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Record a marker (provided by caller) for the current C\+TM. This does not change anything about the ctm or clip, but does \char`\"{}name\char`\"{} this matrix value, so it can be referenced by custom effects (who access it by specifying the same name).

Within a save frame, marking with the same name more than once just replaces the previous value. However, between save frames, marking with the same name does not lose the marker in the previous save frame. It is \char`\"{}visible\char`\"{} when the current \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ac98147dc771b47c7353a51e7c171e428}{save()}} is balanced with a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a1da746e87186d5e3fc0b4838f782e1c4}\label{class_sk_canvas_a1da746e87186d5e3fc0b4838f782e1c4}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!peekPixels@{peekPixels}}
\index{peekPixels@{peekPixels}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{peekPixels()}{peekPixels()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Sk\+Canvas\+::peek\+Pixels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_pixmap}{Sk\+Pixmap}} $\ast$}]{pixmap }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns true if \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} has direct access to its pixels.

Pixels are readable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} is raster. Pixels are not readable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is returned from G\+PU surface, returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_document_a79e3acb788004038aef9dccb1e221160}{Sk\+Document\+::begin\+Page}}, returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture_recorder_a197a4390057dac85b24c0fa35b905d06}{Sk\+Picture\+Recorder\+::begin\+Recording}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is the base of a utility class like Debug\+Canvas.

pixmap is valid only while \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is in scope and unchanged. Any \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_surface}{Sk\+Surface}} call may invalidate the pixmap values.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pixmap} & storage for pixel state if pixels are readable; otherwise, ignored \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} has direct access to pixels
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!readPixels@{readPixels}}
\index{readPixels@{readPixels}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{readPixels()}{readPixels()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Sk\+Canvas\+::read\+Pixels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} \&}]{bitmap,  }\item[{int}]{srcX,  }\item[{int}]{srcY }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} of pixels from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} into bitmap. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip are ignored.

Source \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (srcX, srcY) and (\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.width(), \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.height()). Destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (0, 0) and (bitmap.\+width(), bitmap.\+height()). Copies each readable pixel intersecting both rectangles, without scaling, converting to bitmap.\+color\+Type() and bitmap.\+alpha\+Type() if required.

Pixels are readable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} is raster, or backed by a G\+PU. Pixels are not readable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_document_a79e3acb788004038aef9dccb1e221160}{Sk\+Document\+::begin\+Page}}, returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture_recorder_a197a4390057dac85b24c0fa35b905d06}{Sk\+Picture\+Recorder\+::begin\+Recording}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is the base of a utility class like Debug\+Canvas.

Caller must allocate pixel storage in bitmap if needed.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} values are converted only if Sk\+Color\+Type and Sk\+Alpha\+Type do not match. Only pixels within both source and destination rectangles are copied. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} pixels outside \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} intersection are unchanged.

Pass negative values for srcX or srcY to offset pixels across or down bitmap.

Does not copy, and returns false if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Source and destination rectangles do not intersect.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels could not be converted to bitmap.\+color\+Type() or bitmap.\+alpha\+Type().
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels are not readable; for instance, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is document-\/based.
\item bitmap pixels could not be allocated.
\item bitmap.\+row\+Bytes() is too small to contain one row of pixels.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em bitmap} & storage for pixels copied from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} \\
\hline
{\em srcX} & offset into readable pixels on x-\/axis; may be negative \\
\hline
{\em srcY} & offset into readable pixels on y-\/axis; may be negative \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if pixels were copied
\end{DoxyReturn}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_readPixels_3}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+read\+Pixels\+\_\+3}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_af267c56757f886aaae2d0876161141b1}\label{class_sk_canvas_af267c56757f886aaae2d0876161141b1}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!readPixels@{readPixels}}
\index{readPixels@{readPixels}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{readPixels()}{readPixels()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Sk\+Canvas\+::read\+Pixels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_image_info}{Sk\+Image\+Info}} \&}]{dst\+Info,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst\+Pixels,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+Row\+Bytes,  }\item[{int}]{srcX,  }\item[{int}]{srcY }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} of pixels from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} into dst\+Pixels. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip are ignored.

Source \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (srcX, srcY) and (\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.width(), \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.height()). Destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (0, 0) and (dst\+Info.\+width(), dst\+Info.\+height()). Copies each readable pixel intersecting both rectangles, without scaling, converting to dst\+Info.\+color\+Type() and dst\+Info.\+alpha\+Type() if required.

Pixels are readable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} is raster, or backed by a G\+PU. Pixels are not readable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_document_a79e3acb788004038aef9dccb1e221160}{Sk\+Document\+::begin\+Page}}, returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture_recorder_a197a4390057dac85b24c0fa35b905d06}{Sk\+Picture\+Recorder\+::begin\+Recording}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is the base of a utility class like Debug\+Canvas.

The destination pixel storage must be allocated by the caller.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_pixel}{Pixel}} values are converted only if Sk\+Color\+Type and Sk\+Alpha\+Type do not match. Only pixels within both source and destination rectangles are copied. dst\+Pixels contents outside \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} intersection are unchanged.

Pass negative values for srcX or srcY to offset pixels across or down destination.

Does not copy, and returns false if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Source and destination rectangles do not intersect.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels could not be converted to dst\+Info.\+color\+Type() or dst\+Info.\+alpha\+Type().
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels are not readable; for instance, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is document-\/based.
\item dst\+Row\+Bytes is too small to contain one row of pixels.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dst\+Info} & width, height, Sk\+Color\+Type, and Sk\+Alpha\+Type of dst\+Pixels \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Pixels} & storage for pixels; dst\+Info.\+height() times dst\+Row\+Bytes, or larger \\
\hline
{\em dst\+Row\+Bytes} & size of one destination row; dst\+Info.\+width() times pixel size, or larger \\
\hline
{\em srcX} & offset into readable pixels on x-\/axis; may be negative \\
\hline
{\em srcY} & offset into readable pixels on y-\/axis; may be negative \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

true if pixels were copied 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a7a0e7a8560bf845ee9e30f6da722dcdf}\label{class_sk_canvas_a7a0e7a8560bf845ee9e30f6da722dcdf}}
