\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{readPixels()}{readPixels()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Sk\+Canvas\+::read\+Pixels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_pixmap}{Sk\+Pixmap}} \&}]{pixmap,  }\item[{int}]{srcX,  }\item[{int}]{srcY }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} of pixels from \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} into pixmap. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip are ignored.

Source \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (srcX, srcY) and (\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.width(), \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.height()). Destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (0, 0) and (pixmap.\+width(), pixmap.\+height()). Copies each readable pixel intersecting both rectangles, without scaling, converting to pixmap.\+color\+Type() and pixmap.\+alpha\+Type() if required.

Pixels are readable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} is raster, or backed by a G\+PU. Pixels are not readable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_document_a79e3acb788004038aef9dccb1e221160}{Sk\+Document\+::begin\+Page}}, returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture_recorder_a197a4390057dac85b24c0fa35b905d06}{Sk\+Picture\+Recorder\+::begin\+Recording}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is the base of a utility class like Debug\+Canvas.

Caller must allocate pixel storage in pixmap if needed.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_pixel}{Pixel}} values are converted only if Sk\+Color\+Type and Sk\+Alpha\+Type do not match. Only pixels within both source and destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} are copied. pixmap pixels contents outside \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} intersection are unchanged.

Pass negative values for srcX or srcY to offset pixels across or down pixmap.

Does not copy, and returns false if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Source and destination rectangles do not intersect.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels could not be converted to pixmap.\+color\+Type() or pixmap.\+alpha\+Type().
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels are not readable; for instance, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is document-\/based.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_pixmap}{Sk\+Pixmap}} pixels could not be allocated.
\item pixmap.\+row\+Bytes() is too small to contain one row of pixels.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resetMatrix()}{resetMatrix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::reset\+Matrix (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} to the identity matrix. Any prior matrix state is overwritten.

example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_resetMatrix}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+reset\+Matrix}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}\label{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!restore@{restore}}
\index{restore@{restore}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{restore()}{restore()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::restore (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Removes changes to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip since \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} state was last saved. The state is removed from the stack.

Does nothing if the stack is empty.

example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@AutoCanvasRestore_restore}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Auto\+Canvas\+Restore\+\_\+restore}}

example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_restore}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+restore}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_aae519c51173be795b59f4f4e10c67b9d}\label{class_sk_canvas_aae519c51173be795b59f4f4e10c67b9d}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!restoreToCount@{restoreToCount}}
\index{restoreToCount@{restoreToCount}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{restoreToCount()}{restoreToCount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::restore\+To\+Count (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{save\+Count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Restores state to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip values when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ac98147dc771b47c7353a51e7c171e428}{save()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a06bd76ce35082366bb6b8e6dfcb6f435}{save\+Layer()}}, save\+Layer\+Preserve\+L\+C\+D\+Text\+Requests(), or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a853514477dff62c15ced03f5141b2eb7}{save\+Layer\+Alpha()}} returned save\+Count.

Does nothing if save\+Count is greater than state stack count. Restores state to initial values if save\+Count is less than or equal to one.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em save\+Count} & depth of state stack to restore\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_restoreToCount}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+restore\+To\+Count}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_aaad49aba3b0c320915004e3c420a2780}\label{class_sk_canvas_aaad49aba3b0c320915004e3c420a2780}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!rotate@{rotate}}
\index{rotate@{rotate}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rotate()}{rotate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::rotate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{degrees }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Rotates \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} by degrees. Positive degrees rotates clockwise.

Mathematically, replaces \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} with a rotation matrix premultiplied with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.

This has the effect of rotating the drawing by degrees before transforming the result with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em degrees} & amount to rotate, in degrees\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_rotate}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+rotate}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a2f8897bee82cec6382b21425b5f7580d}\label{class_sk_canvas_a2f8897bee82cec6382b21425b5f7580d}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!rotate@{rotate}}
\index{rotate@{rotate}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{rotate()}{rotate()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::rotate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{degrees,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{px,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{py }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Rotates \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} by degrees about a point at (px, py). Positive degrees rotates clockwise.

Mathematically, constructs a rotation matrix; premultiplies the rotation matrix by a translation matrix; then replaces \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} with the resulting matrix premultiplied with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.

This has the effect of rotating the drawing about a given point before transforming the result with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em degrees} & amount to rotate, in degrees \\
\hline
{\em px} & x-\/axis value of the point to rotate about \\
\hline
{\em py} & y-\/axis value of the point to rotate about\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_rotate_2}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+rotate\+\_\+2}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_ac98147dc771b47c7353a51e7c171e428}\label{class_sk_canvas_ac98147dc771b47c7353a51e7c171e428}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!save@{save}}
\index{save@{save}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{save()}{save()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Sk\+Canvas\+::save (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Saves \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip. Calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}} discards changes to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip, restoring the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip to their state when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ac98147dc771b47c7353a51e7c171e428}{save()}} was called.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a314ca6b7393639642f44a93b2df63fdb}{translate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb01075c3bfab15fc3ded619961dfc15}{scale()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aaad49aba3b0c320915004e3c420a2780}{rotate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_af5049d341b5efe7a5f90207eb2f63641}{skew()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb493a60db8ccd84abbaa26fb9506bcf}{concat()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ad07eb6c080bf2dbc8325e0d12d884915}{set\+Matrix()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aba129108fc68dca01850faf73d5db148}{reset\+Matrix()}}. Clip may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_afcefd4d2ac745ad086fd62f30bbd8564}{clip\+R\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_abc79bd478516f398c31ae9f501154184}{clip\+Path()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8e3773e18ab060b7bb4e1cfc769fb07b}{clip\+Region()}}.

Saved \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} state is put on a stack; multiple calls to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ac98147dc771b47c7353a51e7c171e428}{save()}} should be balance by an equal number of calls to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}}.

Call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aae519c51173be795b59f4f4e10c67b9d}{restore\+To\+Count()}} with result to restore this and subsequent saves.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
depth of saved stack
\end{DoxyReturn}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_save}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+save}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a41aa2893a587e4a371342d7ff809b0d5}\label{class_sk_canvas_a41aa2893a587e4a371342d7ff809b0d5}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!saveLayer@{saveLayer}}
\index{saveLayer@{saveLayer}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{saveLayer()}{saveLayer()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Sk\+Canvas\+::save\+Layer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_canvas_1_1_save_layer_rec}{Save\+Layer\+Rec}} \&}]{layer\+Rec }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Saves \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip, and allocates \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} for subsequent drawing.

Calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}} discards changes to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip, and blends \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} with alpha opacity onto the prior layer.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a314ca6b7393639642f44a93b2df63fdb}{translate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb01075c3bfab15fc3ded619961dfc15}{scale()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aaad49aba3b0c320915004e3c420a2780}{rotate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_af5049d341b5efe7a5f90207eb2f63641}{skew()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb493a60db8ccd84abbaa26fb9506bcf}{concat()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ad07eb6c080bf2dbc8325e0d12d884915}{set\+Matrix()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aba129108fc68dca01850faf73d5db148}{reset\+Matrix()}}. Clip may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_afcefd4d2ac745ad086fd62f30bbd8564}{clip\+R\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_abc79bd478516f398c31ae9f501154184}{clip\+Path()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8e3773e18ab060b7bb4e1cfc769fb07b}{clip\+Region()}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_canvas_1_1_save_layer_rec}{Save\+Layer\+Rec}} contains the state used to create the layer.

Call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aae519c51173be795b59f4f4e10c67b9d}{restore\+To\+Count()}} with returned value to restore this and subsequent saves.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em layer\+Rec} & layer state \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
depth of save state stack before this call was made.
\end{DoxyReturn}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_saveLayer_3}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+save\+Layer\+\_\+3}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a8ba500cff0ee0035ea9aee097c6d5f00}\label{class_sk_canvas_a8ba500cff0ee0035ea9aee097c6d5f00}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!saveLayer@{saveLayer}}
\index{saveLayer@{saveLayer}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{saveLayer()}{saveLayer()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Sk\+Canvas\+::save\+Layer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} \&}]{bounds,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} $\ast$}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Saves \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip, and allocates a \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} for subsequent drawing. Calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}} discards changes to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip, and draws the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a314ca6b7393639642f44a93b2df63fdb}{translate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb01075c3bfab15fc3ded619961dfc15}{scale()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aaad49aba3b0c320915004e3c420a2780}{rotate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_af5049d341b5efe7a5f90207eb2f63641}{skew()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb493a60db8ccd84abbaa26fb9506bcf}{concat()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ad07eb6c080bf2dbc8325e0d12d884915}{set\+Matrix()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aba129108fc68dca01850faf73d5db148}{reset\+Matrix()}}. Clip may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_afcefd4d2ac745ad086fd62f30bbd8564}{clip\+R\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_abc79bd478516f398c31ae9f501154184}{clip\+Path()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8e3773e18ab060b7bb4e1cfc769fb07b}{clip\+Region()}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} bounds suggests but does not define the layer size. To clip drawing to a specific rectangle, use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}.

Optional \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint applies alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and Sk\+Blend\+Mode when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}} is called.

Call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aae519c51173be795b59f4f4e10c67b9d}{restore\+To\+Count()}} with returned value to restore this and subsequent saves.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em bounds} & hint to limit the size of layer; may be nullptr \\
\hline
{\em paint} & graphics state for layer; may be nullptr \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
depth of saved stack 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Sk\+Canvas\+::save\+Layer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} $\ast$}]{bounds,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} $\ast$}]{paint }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}} discards changes to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip, and draws the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a314ca6b7393639642f44a93b2df63fdb}{translate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb01075c3bfab15fc3ded619961dfc15}{scale()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aaad49aba3b0c320915004e3c420a2780}{rotate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_af5049d341b5efe7a5f90207eb2f63641}{skew()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb493a60db8ccd84abbaa26fb9506bcf}{concat()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ad07eb6c080bf2dbc8325e0d12d884915}{set\+Matrix()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aba129108fc68dca01850faf73d5db148}{reset\+Matrix()}}. Clip may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_afcefd4d2ac745ad086fd62f30bbd8564}{clip\+R\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_abc79bd478516f398c31ae9f501154184}{clip\+Path()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8e3773e18ab060b7bb4e1cfc769fb07b}{clip\+Region()}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} bounds suggests but does not define the \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} size. To clip drawing to a specific rectangle, use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}.

Optional \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_paint}{Sk\+Paint}} paint applies alpha, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_color_filter}{Sk\+Color\+Filter}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_image_filter}{Sk\+Image\+Filter}}, and Sk\+Blend\+Mode when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}} is called.

Call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aae519c51173be795b59f4f4e10c67b9d}{restore\+To\+Count()}} with returned value to restore this and subsequent saves.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{saveLayerAlpha()}{saveLayerAlpha()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int Sk\+Canvas\+::save\+Layer\+Alpha (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} $\ast$}]{bounds,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_sk_types_8h_a6882636f582abdb2a130b7e5ff38aa83}{U8\+C\+PU}}}]{alpha }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Saves \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip, and allocates \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} for subsequent drawing.

Calling \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a2c68ed85badf62be77bb862b02dd4961}{restore()}} discards changes to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip, and blends layer with alpha opacity onto prior layer.

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a314ca6b7393639642f44a93b2df63fdb}{translate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb01075c3bfab15fc3ded619961dfc15}{scale()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aaad49aba3b0c320915004e3c420a2780}{rotate()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_af5049d341b5efe7a5f90207eb2f63641}{skew()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb493a60db8ccd84abbaa26fb9506bcf}{concat()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_ad07eb6c080bf2dbc8325e0d12d884915}{set\+Matrix()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aba129108fc68dca01850faf73d5db148}{reset\+Matrix()}}. Clip may be changed by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_afcefd4d2ac745ad086fd62f30bbd8564}{clip\+R\+Rect()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_abc79bd478516f398c31ae9f501154184}{clip\+Path()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a8e3773e18ab060b7bb4e1cfc769fb07b}{clip\+Region()}}.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} bounds suggests but does not define layer size. To clip drawing to a specific rectangle, use \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_a193511e463259ceacfe0e4cf1be1393f}{clip\+Rect()}}.

alpha of zero is fully transparent, 255 is fully opaque.

Call \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aae519c51173be795b59f4f4e10c67b9d}{restore\+To\+Count()}} with returned value to restore this and subsequent saves.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{scale()}{scale()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::scale (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{sx,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{sy }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Scales \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} by sx on the x-\/axis and sy on the y-\/axis.

Mathematically, replaces \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} with a scale matrix premultiplied with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.

This has the effect of scaling the drawing by (sx, sy) before transforming the result with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sx} & amount to scale on x-\/axis \\
\hline
{\em sy} & amount to scale on y-\/axis\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_scale}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+scale}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_ad07eb6c080bf2dbc8325e0d12d884915}\label{class_sk_canvas_ad07eb6c080bf2dbc8325e0d12d884915}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!setMatrix@{setMatrix}}
\index{setMatrix@{setMatrix}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setMatrix()}{setMatrix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::set\+Matrix (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_m44}{Sk\+M44}} \&}]{matrix }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Replaces \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} with matrix. Unlike \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_adb493a60db8ccd84abbaa26fb9506bcf}{concat()}}, any prior matrix state is overwritten.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em matrix} & matrix to copy, replacing existing \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_setMatrix}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+set\+Matrix}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_af5049d341b5efe7a5f90207eb2f63641}\label{class_sk_canvas_af5049d341b5efe7a5f90207eb2f63641}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!skew@{skew}}
\index{skew@{skew}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{skew()}{skew()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::skew (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{sx,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{sy }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Skews \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} by sx on the x-\/axis and sy on the y-\/axis. A positive value of sx skews the drawing right as y-\/axis values increase; a positive value of sy skews the drawing down as x-\/axis values increase.

Mathematically, replaces \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} with a skew matrix premultiplied with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.

This has the effect of skewing the drawing by (sx, sy) before transforming the result with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\end{DoxyParams}

Returns the global clip as a region. If the clip contains AA, then only the bounds of the clip may be returned. \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a314ca6b7393639642f44a93b2df63fdb}\label{class_sk_canvas_a314ca6b7393639642f44a93b2df63fdb}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!translate@{translate}}
\index{translate@{translate}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{translate()}{translate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Sk\+Canvas\+::translate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{dx,  }\item[{Sk\+Scalar}]{dy }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Translates \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} by dx along the x-\/axis and dy along the y-\/axis.

Mathematically, replaces \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} with a translation matrix premultiplied with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.

This has the effect of moving the drawing by (dx, dy) before transforming the result with \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}}.

{\em dy} & distance to translate on y-\/axis\\

\end{DoxyParams}

\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!writePixels@{writePixels}}
\index{writePixels@{writePixels}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writePixels()}{writePixels()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Sk\+Canvas\+::write\+Pixels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_bitmap}{Sk\+Bitmap}} \&}]{bitmap,  }\item[{int}]{x,  }\item[{int}]{y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} from pixels to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip are ignored. Source \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (0, 0) and (bitmap.\+width(), bitmap.\+height()).

Destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (x, y) and (\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.width(), \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.height()).

Copies each readable pixel intersecting both rectangles, without scaling, converting to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.color\+Type() and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.alpha\+Type() if required.

Pixels are writable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} is raster, or backed by a G\+PU. Pixels are not writable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_document_a79e3acb788004038aef9dccb1e221160}{Sk\+Document\+::begin\+Page}}, returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture_recorder_a197a4390057dac85b24c0fa35b905d06}{Sk\+Picture\+Recorder\+::begin\+Recording}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is the base of a utility class like Debug\+Canvas.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_pixel}{Pixel}} values are converted only if Sk\+Color\+Type and Sk\+Alpha\+Type do not match. Only pixels within both source and destination rectangles are copied. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels outside \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} intersection are unchanged.

Pass negative values for x or y to offset pixels to the left or above \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels.

Does not copy, and returns false if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Source and destination rectangles do not intersect.
\item bitmap does not have allocated pixels.
\item bitmap pixels could not be converted to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.color\+Type() or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.alpha\+Type().
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels are not writable; for instance, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is document based.
\item bitmap pixels are inaccessible; for instance, bitmap wraps a texture.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em bitmap} & contains pixels copied to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} \\
\hline
{\em x} & offset into \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} writable pixels on x-\/axis; may be negative \\
\hline
{\em y} & offset into \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} writable pixels on y-\/axis; may be negative \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if pixels were written to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}
\end{DoxyReturn}
example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@Canvas_writePixels_2}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+Canvas\+\_\+write\+Pixels\+\_\+2}} example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@State_Stack_a}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+State\+\_\+\+Stack\+\_\+a}} example\+: \href{https://fiddle.skia.org/c/@State_Stack_b}{\texttt{ https\+://fiddle.\+skia.\+org/c/@\+State\+\_\+\+Stack\+\_\+b}} \mbox{\Hypertarget{class_sk_canvas_a4a65fff01806bf2381aec2d81485e773}\label{class_sk_canvas_a4a65fff01806bf2381aec2d81485e773}} 
\index{SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}!writePixels@{writePixels}}
\index{writePixels@{writePixels}!SkCanvas@{SkCanvas}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writePixels()}{writePixels()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool Sk\+Canvas\+::write\+Pixels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_image_info}{Sk\+Image\+Info}} \&}]{info,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{pixels,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{row\+Bytes,  }\item[{int}]{x,  }\item[{int}]{y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copies \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} from pixels to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_matrix}{Sk\+Matrix}} and clip are ignored. Source \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (0, 0) and (info.\+width(), info.\+height()). Destination \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} corners are (x, y) and (\mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.width(), \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.height()).

Copies each readable pixel intersecting both rectangles, without scaling, converting to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.color\+Type() and \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.alpha\+Type() if required.

Pixels are writable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_base_device}{Sk\+Base\+Device}} is raster, or backed by a G\+PU. Pixels are not writable when \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_document_a79e3acb788004038aef9dccb1e221160}{Sk\+Document\+::begin\+Page}}, returned by \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_picture_recorder_a197a4390057dac85b24c0fa35b905d06}{Sk\+Picture\+Recorder\+::begin\+Recording}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is the base of a utility class like Debug\+Canvas.

\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_pixel}{Pixel}} values are converted only if Sk\+Color\+Type and Sk\+Alpha\+Type do not match. Only pixels within both source and destination rectangles are copied. \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels outside \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sk_rect}{Sk\+Rect}} intersection are unchanged.

Pass negative values for x or y to offset pixels to the left or above \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels.

Does not copy, and returns false if\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Source and destination rectangles do not intersect.
\item pixels could not be converted to \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.color\+Type() or \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas_aef8a74b34be1cefa29eac1ab7a1c6727}{image\+Info()}}.alpha\+Type().
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} pixels are not writable; for instance, \mbox{\hyperlink{class_sk_canvas}{Sk\+Canvas}} is document-\/based.
\item row\+Bytes is too small to contain one row of pixels.
\end{DoxyItemize}
